Our favorite no frills, hands down, best tasting, authentic Mexican food restaurant in the area. Besides the great food the staff is friendly and will always accommodate some of our special, off-menu requests.

I went there yesterday and the store was actually a lot smaller on the inside than what it looks like from the street. It does have a smallish collection of comic books, but that will change over time. It has a number of other collectibles, including a few Magic the Gathering packs of the recent sets.

<Rate>5< /Rate><Review>There are only a few bakeries where originality, creativity, and good food come together. Rolling-Out Cafe is one of these few. After my 1st visit several years ago when my friend told me about it, I've gone back many times.

My most favorites are the egg tarts and the quiche. Their quiche is the best I've tasted so far. The mini egg tarts have just the right sweetness; and are perfect for enjoying alone or for sharing. Sometimes if I go late during the date, I might be able to find one or two left if I'm lucky. I'm so glad there are more flavors now--original, cream cheese, sweet potato, chocolate, & bacon. And they are all delicious.

Other food are also good, like the sausage roll, croissants, star-shaped donut (kids would love this), etc. The rosemary mac and cheese is definitely recommended too. It's made to order, and when it's baked, the aroma fills the whole cafe.

During my recent visits, I was happy to find that they have a holiday special--a more sophisticated version of the traditional sweet potato pie. It's made with rum, and can be made as smaller individual pies if ordered in advance. I brought them to a party, and whoever tried it just loved it.

Thank you for making such good food available for people to enjoy!<//Review><Pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOxc6tjjElC4W9Wcog1tM4yovbldXWjuscl7Ni8=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]</Pictures><response>None< /response>< GmapID>

< review>
We picked up breakfast here on a Sunday morning on our way to the zoo, and had a positive experience!  Tasty food, friendly service, and a Covid-safe set up.

We texted our order in advance, which is a nice option to have.

We ordered the following:

1) 1 breakfast sandwich with egg and cheese - great, with excellent bread; the sandwich was a bit saltier than I would have preferred

2) 2 breakfast sandwiches with egg, bacon, greens, and tomatoes - pretty good, with tasty aioli, though a bit difficult to eat (it would have nice if the bread was bigger)

3) mini Croissant - good; nice they had a mini version

4) Americanos - not very good; unfortunately, I wouldn't come here for the coffee

There was one person working and he was very polite, professional, and efficient.

I appreciated the fact that they accept Apple Pay for payment.

We'd love to return here for breakfast sandwiches again!<//review>

<Time>1451861862288<//Time><Rate>5<//Rate>< text>
Rolling out cafe is an amazing place to find cinnamon rolls in the city!
The pastries have a very authentic home made taste.
My favorites are the sweet potato cinnamon roll and the Hawaiian sticky bun.
The coffee is simple, but not overpriced. Could use a little fancier beans and brewing methods, but that would cost more. It would be nice to have two options, simple coffee, and fancy coffee.
The environment is very home-feeling. Don't forget to check out the upstairs. It's the perfect place to invite somebody to study with or study alone. Since nobody can pass through, it's very safe and cozy up there. There are also really cozy chairs on the ground floor too of course. There are a couple chairs outside, and there will be a sidewalk parklet coming soon. Can't wait for that with warmer weather later in the year.<//text>

<rating>5<//rating><user_name>Sherry Li< /user_name><Pictures>None< /Pictures><Resp>None< /Resp><Date>1429562209695</Date><UserId.>101220706149966390072<//UserId.>< gmap_id>
0x808f7d84c97ee8f5:0x1f9c8fe78c3130b6</gmap_id>
< Review>
Cute and unassuming cafe in Outer Sunset along the Taraval vein. You wouldn't know that some of the best pastries are being churned out here.

The owner is super nice. A chemist in his former life, now he bakes and mans the storefront. He has some interesting items on sale - bacon egg tart, sweet potato cinnamon roll, to name a couple. I asked for his recommendations and he gave me BOGO because I couldn't choose between the sweet potato cinnamon roll and the hawaiian sticky bun. And I'm glad he did, because both tasted great. And to his instruction, both can be reheated in the microwave or oven if you, for some reason, can't consume them right away.

If you're waiting for some take out from one of the many dumpling holes in the three block radius, come here for some dessert! I guarantee that you'll like the pastries here more than the dumplings ;) Because P.S. the dumplings in this area are overhyped.<//Review>

<Review>FITS VEHICLES WITH BARN DOORS!
Let me start by stating that I have ordered LED tail lights from 2 other companies that did NOT fit my Suburban with cargo (barn) doors. The issue is the narrow clearance in the bottom of the lights due to the door hinge (for barn doors). The other LED tail lights that I ordered were designed with a back up light at the bottom which did not allow for enough clearance to fit a vehicle WITH barn doors.
YOUR item, 03-CD2000LED DOES fit a Suburban/Tahoe/Yukon with barn doors! They are designed with the back up light in the CENTER of the light, keeping the tail light narrow at the very bottom. <userid>106805279149940203804< /userid>< Text>
Amazing, fast service and great looking products.
I ordered LED projector headlights for my 2015 Camaro and they were delivered before I had even received a tracking number for them. The confirmation email said 'expect 3-5 business days' or something like that, but my order was at my front door the next day. The headlights didn't come with any installation instructions, which I emailed the support team about. However, by the time they got back to me later that day, I had already finished the installation because it was so easy. Literally all I had to do was look at the headlight housing to figure out what to do. If you can tell the difference between red and black wires, you can instal these headlights with no instructions whatsoever. As far as the headlights themselves, they are noticeably better than factory halogen bulbs, but aren't so stupid bright that you'll blind oncoming traffic. Perfectly in between. I could not be happier with my order; it was prompt, easy to instal and looks awesome.</Text>

These are falsely marketed as "plug and play." I ordered aftermarket LED projector headlights specific to my Jetta mk6 ('11-'14).  This product does not match depiction, nor description in linked video content.. The secondary electrical fitment does not match OEM electrical terminals. This would require electrical re-wiring. The received product does not have the same wiring as the advertised product.

The only information guide included with the product is written in incoherent broken English.

Contacted ProTuning via email 3/26. l Will update review when fixed.

*Update:
- The load resistors fell off the assembly. They get extremely hot, and the manufacturer didn‚Äôt use a proper high temperature adhesive or a proper mount location. Furthermore, the manufacturer thought it would be wise to install a device that reaches 260 degrees Fahrenheit on a thermoplastic.
-Load resistors were not even the correct resistance to simulate the OEM voltage and prevent the computer from throwing a bulb-out code.
-This clear plastic part of the light assembly chipped from wear in the natural elements, after just under a year.
-The assemblies wasn‚Äôt properly sealed by the manufacturer from moisture.
-The electrical elements ultimately failed.
-The OEM assemblies were reinstalled and the problems disappeared.
-No warranty.

Conclusion: Complete waste of money. Extremely cheap, inferior, poorly-manufactured product. ProTuning will not refund/exchange, unless product has not been installed.<//review>
